婕伊舰桥问答

返回舰桥问答目录

Smuggler

条件选项

  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“我还在等着你解释呢，婕伊。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“知道了这些事情之后，我只要一想到要把你留在身边，就觉得恶心。赶紧从我眼前消失！”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；[杀死她]“你要为你所做的一切付出代价！”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“告诉我你真正的过去吧。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected、Etude、Quest；“你之前不是说，等咱们回到藏身处之后，你要喝个烂醉如泥吗？”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“再给我讲一次你的故事吧。”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“你的肺怎么样了？”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected、Etude；“你就没想过告诉我真相，哪怕一次也好？毕竟，我不仅仅只是你的赞助人。”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“你之前真的去找我了吗？你是想救我一命吗？”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“丹罗克说你和一个叫‘悯慈’的人勾结，这个‘悯慈’是什么人？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你现在尽可以放纵。不过，等我们回到科罗努斯扩区之后，你要重新戴上你公主的面具，不要让我的名字蒙羞。”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“这种粗鄙的举止确实更符合你卑劣的性格。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“咱们该如何离开这里，你有什么想法吗？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“该说的话都已经说完了，回去办正事吧。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；[离开]“保持警惕，我需要你的协助。”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“婕伊，你知不知道我的伺服头骨为什么开始说怪话了？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你和骗术师科尔好像关系很好。他掉了脑袋，真令人遗憾。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你之前是不是打算和我谈生意？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我可以帮你弄到行商执照。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我听说你和卡西娅闹翻了？你甚至威胁说要杀了她？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你和我讲过你丰富多彩的过去，婕伊，但我觉得那些故事恐怕并不全是真的……”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“你看起来不太像那种常见的走私者。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“再和我说说你的过去吧。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你也是卡斯巴利卡的强盗男爵吗？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你是怎么成为卡斯巴利卡的代理人的？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你留在落脚港的帮派要怎么办？你相信他们吗？”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected、Etude；“请原谅我的窥探，但尊贵的公主，请问你的真心是否已被某个幸运的先生夺走？”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“我很欣赏你的浪漫品味，很好。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“算了吧，这种激情的游戏太复杂了，不适合我。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“我并没有把你当成玩物，我就是很喜欢你……”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你什么时候才愿意来我的房间？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“我邀请你来我的房间。”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“晚上来我的房间，穿上我送给你的新礼服，我想好好欣赏欣赏你。”
  • 显示条件：Companion；“你好像对阿洁塔相当钟意，我说得对吗？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“这个选择要由你自己来做，婕伊。我所能做的，便是支持你的选择。”
  • 显示条件：AnswerSelected；“怎么小小的商业问题都让你这么紧张？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“阴影男爵吗？若能得到这样的盟友，肯定不是什么坏事。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你拥有足够的实力，可以成为卡斯巴利卡的阴影男爵，活跃于科罗努斯扩区。”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“有了帝国官方行商执照，你想做什么都可以！”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你觉得怎么合适就怎么办吧。”

选项索引

  • “我还在等着你解释呢，婕伊。”
  • “也就是说，你曾是帝国卫队中的一员？”
  • “你是怎么和卡斯巴利卡扯上关系的？”
  • “也就是说，你还是个逃兵？”
  • “我现在知道你肺里的植入物是怎么来的了，但那只手又是怎么回事？”
  • “我明白了。”
  • “你是从哪里学会读书写字的？”
  • “至少婕伊这个名字是真的吧？”
  • “有什么事情你对我说过实话吗，婕伊？”
  • “知道了这些事情之后，我只要一想到要把你留在身边，就觉得恶心。赶紧从我眼前消失！”
  • [[杀死她]“你要为你所做的一切付出代价！”](#choice-01-011)
  • “我明白了，谢谢你回答我的问题。”
  • “告诉我你真正的过去吧。”
  • “你之前不是说，等咱们回到藏身处之后，你要喝个烂醉如泥吗？”
  • “再给我讲一次你的故事吧。”
  • “你的肺怎么样了？”
  • “你就没想过告诉我真相，哪怕一次也好？毕竟，我不仅仅只是你的赞助人。”
  • “你之前为什么没有告诉我真相？”
  • “我坚持，从现在开始，我们之间要保持绝对坦诚。”
  • [[耸肩]“如果你想知道，我看待这一切的态度有没有变，那我想说没有。你从来没有变过，我对你的感觉也没有变过。”](#choice-01-020)
  • “我无权评判你。如果换做是我，我也希望我的爱人能把我当成一位王子/公主，而不是下巢的渣滓。”
  • “你之前真的去找我了吗？你是想救我一命吗？”

  • “你本可以当个甩手掌柜，坐享其成，可你为什么要踏上虚空舰，过着充满危险的生活？”

问答正文

婕伊疲惫地叹了口气，直直地看着你。“好吧，大人，你尽管问吧。我会实话实说，不打算再狡辩了。”
With a weary sigh, Jae gives you a hard stare. "Well, Your Lordship/Ladyship, ask away. I'll tell it like it is. I'm not going to try to wriggle out of it."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“我还在等着你解释呢，婕伊。”
"I am still waiting for an explanation, Jae."

选项 Choices

婕伊不以为然地耸了耸肩。“落脚港的那群人是我唯一的家人，亲爱的。骗术师双胞胎和别的下层人，他们说话直截了当，像狗一样忠诚……有时候也像破旧的刀柄一样迟钝。”
Jae gives an indifferent shrug. "The folks on Footfall are my only family, shereen. The Trickster Twins and the rest of the rabble. Plain-talking and loyal as dogs... And sometimes as dull as the pommel of a worn-out blade."

  • 选择 Choice

“也就是说，你曾是帝国卫队中的一员？”
"So you used to be in the Imperial Guard?"

“海达利下士报到，长官！”婕伊向你敬了个礼，但这愚蠢的举止却让她变得闷闷不乐。“我这辈子都再也不想碰星界军的那堆狗屎了，亲爱的。我已经从与异形与异端分子的生意中赚到了足够的东西，足够让我用两辈子了。可是……每当提到帝国卫队，我都感觉根本无法真正地从过去中走出来。 那段该死的日子，至今仍把我紧紧地捏在手中。不过这也意味着，我依然记得身为一名渺小的、浑身颤抖的、无足轻重的走卒是什么感觉。正是因为这个原因，我才如此珍惜我如今拥有的一切。”
"Corporal Heydari reporting for duty, sir/ma'am!" Jae salutes you, but the silly playacting only sours her mood. "I've had enough of the Astra Militarum's shit to last a lifetime, shereen. And my body's collected enough souvenirs from run-ins with xenos and heretics to last two lifetimes. Except... when it comes to the Guard, there's no such thing as 'used to be.' That wretched life sank its claws into me good. But that also means I remember what it's like to be a small, shaking, insignificant pawn. And that's why I appreciate what I have now all the more."

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“你是怎么和卡斯巴利卡扯上关系的？”
"How did you get involved with the Kasballica?"

“怎么，你觉得这很困难吗？有一次，我和我在卫队的伙伴溜进了巢都上层，想找间不错的酒吧。那个世界所有的上层人物都聚集在那个地方。还有一次，我们所在的师团被派去守卫另一个巢都世界最高的尖塔……于是我突然就顿悟了，我看到了另一半人都是怎么生活的。我说的‘另一半人’，指的是那些出生时嘴里含着钻石勺子的人，不是屁眼里塞着工兵铲的人。”
"What, you think it's difficult? Once, me and my fellow Guardsmen snuck into the upper city in search of a good watering hole where the high and mighty of that world congregated. Another time our regiment was sent to defend the tallest spires on a hive world... and I had an epiphany. I saw how the other half lives, and by half, I mean the ones born with a diamond spoon in their mouth, instead of an entrenching shovel rammed up their arse."

“于是，我的眼界被打开了，我看到了真相，亲爱的。帝国充满了机会，就算对我这样的人也不例外。诀窍在于弄清楚该去吻谁的手，该去舔谁的靴子，该去掐谁的喉咙，该去踹谁的屁股。于是，我在卫队指挥部里得到了所有人的欢迎。无论他们想要什么，我都可以帮他们弄到……于是，卡斯巴利卡注意到了我。”
"My eyes were opened to the truth, shereen. The Imperium is full of opportunities, even for people like myself. The trick is knowing whose palms to grease, whose boots to lick, whose throat to squeeze, and whose arses to kick. I was very popular with everyone in the Guard command, you see — I'd procure things for them, whatever they wanted... And so the Kasballica took notice."

  • 选择 Choice

“也就是说，你还是个逃兵？”
"So you are a deserter as well?"

“你知道吗，亲爱的？如果我没有下定决心改善我的生活，我现在可能还窝在吱吱嘎嘎的旧船上，与令人厌恶的嘟囔声为伴，从一个世界颠簸到另一个世界。我曾经负责接收过卡斯巴利卡运来的一批……化学品，用来享受肉体欢愉或者类似的东西，你懂的。当时有个大人物，他为了庆祝服役五十周年，举办了一场派对。”
"You know, shereen, I could still be bouncing around from one world to another, holed up on tired old ships with only venal grunts for company, if I hadn't decided I wanted more for my life. I accepted a shipment from the Kasballica of certain... chemicals. You know, for carnal pleasures and the like. Some bigwig was throwing a party to celebrate his fifth decade in the service."

“就是那个时候，我引起了新任政委的注意。我一只手掏着星界军的口袋，另一只手运着卡斯巴利卡的货物。你可以想象，如果那个政委没有先去调查我上面的那些老主顾，我的脑袋会发生什么事情。”婕伊用拇指划过她的金属喉咙，苦笑起来。
"And that's when I caught the attention of the newly arrived Commissar. I was rummaging through the pockets of Astra Militarum with one hand and shuffling the Kasballican cargo with the other. You can imagine what would've happened to my head had the Commissar not started with my higher-ranked patrons." Jae draws a thumb across her metallic throat and chuckles bitterly.

  • 选择 Choice

“我现在知道你肺里的植入物是怎么来的了，但那只手又是怎么回事？”
"That explains the lung implant, but what about the hand?"

“是兽人干的。”婕伊做了个沮丧的手势。“我有些话没说谎，亲爱的。”
"It was Orks." Jae makes a frustrated gesture. "Not everything I say is a lie, shereen."

  • 选择 Choice

“我明白了。”
"I see."

“你明白个——呃，当我没说。”
"Whoop-dee fu— eh, never mind."

  • 选择 Choice

“你是从哪里学会读书写字的？”
"So where did you learn to read and write?"

“啊，读书写字！我的祝福，我的诅咒。只要有贵族来我们的军营里做生意，我就会缠着他们叨叨个不停。我仔细研究仓库里板条箱上的印章，以及每扇门上的封条。我旁观指挥官做文书工作，自愿帮忙……这就是我的学习方式，一步一个脚印。在那之后，识字的能力就成了我通往舒适生活的门票！”婕伊向后甩着肩膀，显然非常自豪。
"Ah, literacy! My blessing and my curse. I nagged every highborn who visited our barracks on their highborn business. I pored over stamps on crates in the warehouse and the seals on every door, watched the commanders do paperwork and volunteered to help... That's how I learned, one step at a time. And then literacy became my ticket to a comfortable life!" Jae sets back her shoulders, obviously very proud of herself.

  • 选择 Choice

“至少婕伊这个名字是真的吧？”
"Is Jae your real name, at least?"

Then he wondered why his neighbour's business failed to make him any more money."

“我不清楚，亲爱的。如你所知，我最近最不想做的事情，就是策划巧妙的计划。不过好消息是，当那个混蛋血伶人忙着在我身上做实验的时候，我从他的实验室里偷走了几件小玩意儿。愿鬼怪吞了那个黑心混蛋的骨头。收下吧，这些东西可能会派上用场。就算没办法帮助我们逃跑，也可以帮我们在这个烂坑里活下来。”
"That's a negative, shereen. Hatching clever plans has been the last thing on my mind recently, you see. But on the bright side, while that ashmag Haemonculus — may the azhi devour that black-souled bag of bones — was busy experimenting on me, I managed to nick a couple of trinkets from his laboratory. Here, they may come in useful, if not for escaping, then at least for surviving in this rotten hole."

“知道了这些事情之后，我只要一想到要把你留在身边，就觉得恶心。赶紧从我眼前消失！”
"After what I have heard, the thought of keeping you by my side makes me sick. Remove yourself from my presence!"

“好吧，这并不令人意外。行商浪人与走私者为伴还算可以接受，可容忍一介平民，一个逃兵成为随行人员？不行，这恐怕太过分了。从现在起，我将尽我所能，不让我卑微的身份玷污你威严的目光。”
"Well, that was predictable. The Rogue Trader is fine with the company of a smuggler, but tolerating a commoner and a deserter in his/her retinue? No, that is a step too far. From now on, I will endeavour not to offend your majestic gaze with my humble person."

“你让我想起某个我认识的人，{name}。他经营着一家商店，经营得很好，但他却嫉妒他的邻居，因为他的邻居赚得更多。于是他杀了邻居，接管了邻居的商店，但他却不怎么喜欢邻居的货物，于是就用他自己的货物换掉了邻居的货物。在那之后，他一直想不通，为什么邻居的店铺没有为他赚来更多的钱。”
"You remind me of a man I once knew, {name}. He had a well-stocked shop but was envious of his neighbour because his store was more profitable. So he killed his neighbour and took over the shop, except he didn't like the goods and quickly replaced them with his own. Then he wondered why his neighbour's business failed to make him any more money."

“换句话说，你并不清楚你想要什么。你把我庇护在你的翅膀之下，把我拖进这座城市，将我从痛苦的死亡中拯救出来，听我吐露心声……而现在，你却要把我赶走！好吧，你爱怎么样就怎么样吧。我要走了，亲爱的。还有，别再来敲我的门了，我的门再也不会为你打开了。”
"In other words, you don't know what you want: you've taken me under your wing, dragged me into this city, saved me from excruciating death, listened to me spilling my guts... And now you're casting me out? Fine, have it your way. I'm leaving, shereen. And don't come knocking on my door ever again — it'll be closed to you."

"Once upon a time, there was a little girl who lived on a sand-covered lump of rock, and the core of that rock contained untold riches for servants of the Imperium. And every day until she turned sixteen, the girl scraped out those riches with her little hands, breaking her back and coughing up her lungs, on behalf of people who had never clapped eyes upon her and who would never know her name."

“家族最小的孩子，注定会成为政治游戏中的筹码，但我不愿意接受这样的命运。我想做出我自己的选择，走我自己的路。当我得知，至高无上的神皇在遥远的星空中注视着几百个其他世界时，我突然意识到艾弗里特之外还有无数世界与无数机遇。我要做的事情，就是打破束缚我的家族纽带，逃出那颗行星——这便是我很久以前做的事情。”
"The youngest child is destined to become a bargaining chip in the family's political games. But I was unwilling to accept such a fate and wanted to choose what to become and which path to follow. When I learned the Exalted One watches over hundreds of other worlds amidst distant stars, I understood there was an entire world of opportunities beyond Efreet. All I had to do was break the familial bonds tying me down and escape the planet — which I did a long time ago."

  • 选择 Choice

“做我们这一行，意味着要认识合适的人与异形，拥有合适的联络人，确保珍贵的货物能顺利交付到我那些不那么珍贵的客户手中。我的智慧包括对人类之敌的充分了解，无论是异形，还是帝国最底层的人渣。此外，我还很了解货物的价格，知道各种各样的文物在落脚港的市场上能卖到多少钱。我可以向你保证，亲爱的，只要我在你身边，哪怕是最狡猾的鬼怪也骗不了你。而且，如果你那深不见底的财富依然无法满足你的渴求，那我所拥有的一切也可以归你所有。”
"My trade means knowing the right people and non-people, having the right connections, and making sure the precious goods find their way into the hands of my no-less-precious customers. My wisdom includes the knowledge of the enemies of Humankind, be they xenos or the lowest scum in the Imperium, as well as the latest knowledge about how much they charge for any particular curio at the Footfall market. Not even the most cunning azhi will deceive you as long as I am with you, shereen — I promise you that. Whatever I have can be yours too — if your unfathomable wealth isn't enough for you already, I mean."

“你在与人类之敌做生意吗？”
"Do you do business with the enemies of Humanity?"

"It has been known to happen. After years of dealing with xenos, I've learned their customs and even got a grasp of their language — except they cringe whenever I start speaking. Arrogant sods! They dislike even our voices, but they never turn away our valuables. Then again, I'm used to seeing sour faces — in this trade, the easily offended go out of business."

"So Vigdis is snooping in on my vox-line..." Jae grins crookedly and shrugs. "I wasn't threatening your Navigator, I didn't even think about it. I was just relaxing in the good company of fragrant amasec, sweet-scented lho, and a handful of new friends from the upper decks... And right in the middle of the fun, the Lady Navigator swoops in and starts jabbering about how her head is about to split from the 'cacophony of colours' coming from our cabin."

“总之长话短说，亲爱的。很不幸，我体会到了你的军官一直在谈论的那些事情。他们说，当那个奥赛罗家族的姑娘不开心的时候，周围每个人都会失去理智，被鬼怪上身。那样的痛苦根本没办法用语言描述……我只记得，当时每个人都蜷缩在角落里，哭的像坏了的电喇叭一样。至于卡西娅……我猜，她被我们衣衫不整的样子吓坏了，你肯定也能想象得到。我们还没搞清楚到底发生了什么事情，那个可怜的小姑娘就跑了。当时的情况非常尴尬……至于那些威胁的话，是吼给参加聚会的某个姑娘听的。是我太蠢了，我邀请她也参加了聚会，结果那个小贱人趁着当时一片混乱，从我眼皮底下偷走了整整一袋麻烟！”
"Long story short, shereen, I had the misfortune of getting a taste of what your officers have been going on about — they say when the Orsellio girl becomes upset, everyone in the vicinity loses their minds and is overtaken by azhi. And it hurt like anything... I can only remember everyone huddling in a corner, wailing like klaxons. As for Cassia... I think Cassia was flustered by the state of our clothes, which were very meagre back then, as you understand. Before I could get my bearings, the poor thing was gone. The whole situation was awkward... As for the threats, they were addressed to one of the girls I'd been foolish enough to invite to our little party. That kaskha used the confusion to pilfer a full pouch of lho from under my nose!"

Jae stops smiling and rubs the bridge of her nose wearily. "Listen, shereen, the giver of happiness and the dearest of my friends... Well, have pity on mine, it has already been gnawed at by the azhi. And if you don't like the sound of that, we'll just go our separate ways, deal?"

All doors are open here — you can become a saint, a mogul, a kingmaker, or anyone you like, really. Here, hard work pays off, unless you're used to lying by the roadside and complaining instead of toiling for the good of your soul, glory, wallet, or whatever floats your boat. “背叛指的是在自己人背后捅刀，但我却在利用敌人来充实帝国的国库。只有金钱才能推动战争的磨盘。帝皇的仆人就在这在虚空的边缘，在这远离神圣泰拉的地方，与敌人进行着永无休止的战斗。他们比以往更加需要我依靠非法手段赚来的黄金，无论是在他们口袋里，还是在他们手中。”
"Betrayal means driving a knife in the back of one of your own. I am using our enemies to enrich the Imperium. Money makes the millstones of war turn, and since the servants of the Emperor are fighting their ceaseless battle even here, at the edge of the void and away from Holy Terra, they need my misbegotten gold more than ever, both in their pockets and in circulation."

"The things we do for profit and gain, right?"

"Emperor be praised! You took the words right out of my mouth."

  • 选择 Choice

"Thank you, shereen. Being able to read and write is chief among them. I didn't escape Efreet to consign myself to such misery. It was literacy that paved my path to copied orders, forged signatures, counterfeited papers... The wonderful things that make the wheels of bureaucracy turn in the right direction."

I do not consider myself rich. I am not rich enough."

“你又何尝不是呢，{name}？”婕伊扬起了眉毛。“我已经厌倦了落脚港没完没了的合同与协议。这种事情我已经干了……多少年？但在这里，在群星之间，无论做什么都像是在刀尖上跳舞。没有什么事情比亚空间跳跃更刺激，更能令我兴奋，更不用提那些危机四伏的行星了。落脚港让我变得越来越脑满肠肥，亲爱的，我可不想变成那个样子。”

婕伊的通讯珠亮了起来，显示有信息传入。她礼貌地朝你点点头，之后移开了目光，认真聆听着传入的信息。在这之后，她的脸色渐渐变得阴沉下来，随后以紧张的动作切断了传输。
Jae's communication device lights up, indicating an incoming message. She gives you a polite nod, looks away, and focuses on the message that is being transmitted to her comm-bead. With each passing moment, her expression darkens. Then she cuts off the transmission with a nervous gesture.

“在那场航行中，指引我的并不是信仰，也不是金光闪闪的饰品。噢，都不是。我意识到了某种力量，那些拥有力量的人们，藏在你发出的刺眼明光之中，亲爱的。这种力量会化为阴影，绕过那些早已过时的律法，维护秩序与光明。我愿意成为那个阴影，亲爱的。或许，我可以成为你的阴影？我不再是卡斯巴利卡犯罪集团的走卒，而会亲自成为科罗努斯扩区的阴影男爵，成为比那些一文不名的管家更加强大、更加可怕的力量。”
"And it was not faith or the glitter of golden baubles that steered me on that voyage, oh no. I realised the power of those who hide in the blinding light of luminaries such as yourself, shereen. The power that lies in being a shadow that upholds order and light by skirting around antiquated laws. I will become that shadow, shereen. Perhaps I will even be your shadow? Not another pawn of the Kasballica Mission, but a Shadow Baron of the Expanse in my own right. A power far more imperious and formidable than any penny-pinching steward."

“王朝的继承人与罪犯一起喝酒，行商浪人与卡斯巴利卡达成交易，几十艘舰船从漫长的航行停下来，来到这里休息。整个帝国还有比这里更美好的地方吗？帝皇对弱小与强大的人们都很仁慈。只要你的脑袋还在脖子上，就肯定能找到赖以为生的手段。如果你打算与帝皇私下谈谈的话，无论你在哪颗小行星上，都能看到至高无上的神皇雕像。你可以尽情祈祷，直到你心满意足为止。”
"Dynasty heirs drink with criminals, Rogue Traders strike deals with the Kasballica, and dozens of ships stop off for a welcome break from a long voyage — is there a more beautiful place in the entire Imperium? The Emperor is merciful to the meek and the powerful alike. There's a job for everyone as long as they have a head on their shoulders. And if you feel like talking to Him in person, the statue of the Exalted One can be seen from any asteroid — you can pray to your heart's content."

  • 选择 Choice

“和我说说卡斯巴利卡犯罪集团的情况吧。”
"Tell me about the Kasballica Mission."

“那是个古老的犯罪集团，起源于卡利西斯星区的第一批定居者。这个集团由阴影中的氏族组成，由强盗男爵掌舵。如果你惹上了他们，你就可能会在科罗努斯扩区中四面树敌，甚至可能连整个帝国境内都是你的敌人。至于他们的代理人，那些人不过是一群无耻、贪婪的人渣。”
"An ancient crime cartel that originated with the first settlers of the Calixis Sector. It is run by shadowy clans with robber barons at the helm. Cross their path, and you risk making enemies all over the Koronus Expanse, or even the entire Imperium. As for the agents, they are just shameless, greedy scum."

“在落脚港，每三个人里就有一个人为卡斯巴利卡做事。不过，这并不意味着那群烂人会团结一心。我曾不止一次遭到陷害，仅仅是因为卡斯巴利卡的某个成员打算压他的竞争对手一头。不过，卡斯巴利卡对客户始终都很慷慨。只要你能承担得起他们的价格，他们便可以为你弄到任何东西，运到你面前。顾客永远是对的，除非顾客碰巧是个二五仔。如果是这种情况……”婕伊叹了口气，举起了手。
"Every third person on Footfall is a Kasballican, but that doesn't mean all that rotten filth is acting together — I've been set up more than once just so some Kasballican can get one over on his rivals. And yet the Kasballica is generous to its customers — if you can afford it. Anything can be obtained, organised, and transported for the right price. The customer is always right, unless they happen to be a rat, in which case..." Jae sighs and throws up her hands.

“在落脚港，这种事情没什么难的。我花了一年的时间为老好人克里斯托工作。他是个勇敢的士兵，和兽人混战的时候丧了命，于是我便接管了他的生意。只要保护好自己的脑袋别掉，把至高无上的神皇放在心里，就有助于迅速认识新的伙伴。到了最后，我聚集了一群诚实而忠诚的人。我仅仅做了几笔成功的交易，就引起了卡斯巴利卡的注意。很快，我便在落脚港安顿下来，将我的智慧传授给我的门徒与下属。到了那个时候，我已经不再需要亲自弄脏手了。”
"It's not hard to do on Footfall. I spent a year working for good old Cristo — he was a brave soldier who gave up the ghost in a scuffle with Orks — and then took over his business. Having a good head on your shoulders and keeping the Exalted One in your heart helps to establish new contacts quickly. Eventually I gathered together a group of honest and loyal people, and it only took a few successful contracts for the Kasballica to take notice. I quickly settled on Footfall and started dispensing my wisdom to my proteges and subordinates — I lost the taste for getting my hands dirty."

“实际上真的很简单，亲爱的。卡斯巴利卡经营着帝国的黑市，为那些能负担得起服务的人提供特别的商品。没错，我指的就是异形造物，包括外星武器与技术设备……有时甚至会包括某些……活着的东西。”

"Unlike the Rogue Traders whose sacred Warrants make them immune even from the laws of the Exalted One, Kasballican agents are used to hiding and covering their tracks. Not even the most cunning azhi will deceive you as long as I am with you, shereen — I promise you that. Whatever I have can be yours too — if your unfathomable wealth isn't enough for you already, I mean."

The sparkle in Jae's dark eyes fades for an instant. "My gang is quite the void beast, shereen, with three heads stemming from a single neck! Kor's untimely demise will not interfere with our mutual business." Jae looks away and continues dryly. "I do feel sorry for his twin, though. Torra has been getting into trouble with her brother since they were kids. Getting out of trouble, too. But not this time."

“不过，干嘛要谈论那些已经不在的人呢，亲爱的？我们还有很多好听的话，要说给那些活着的人呢。比如说，法尔科。”婕伊攥紧了她的钢手，发出了吱吱作响的声音。“我准备把那个坏种串在木桩上，亲爱的，你会亲眼看到的。我要选一条又细又长的木桩，这样他就有更多时间来享受它的滋味了。”
"But why are we talking about the departed, shereen? We must save a few good words for the living. Take Falco, for example." Jae clenches her steel hand until it starts squeaking in protest. Here, hard work pays off, unless you're used to lying by the roadside and complaining instead of toiling for the good of your soul, glory, wallet, or whatever floats your boat. “做我们这一行，意味着要认识合适的人与异形，拥有合适的联络人，确保珍贵的货物能顺利交付到我那些不那么珍贵的客户手中。我的智慧包括对人类之敌的充分了解，无论是异形，还是帝国最底层的人渣。此外，我还很了解货物的价格，知道各种各样的文物在落脚港的市场上能卖到多少钱。我可以向你保证，亲爱的，只要我在你身边，哪怕是最狡猾的鬼怪也骗不了你。而且，如果你那深不见底的财富依然无法满足你的渴求，那我所拥有的一切也可以归你所有。”
"My trade means knowing the right people and non-people, having the right connections, and making sure the precious goods find their way into the hands of my no-less-precious customers. My wisdom includes the knowledge of the enemies of Humankind, be they xenos or the lowest scum in the Imperium, as well as the latest knowledge about how much they charge for any particular curio at the Footfall market. Not even the most cunning azhi will deceive you as long as I am with you, shereen — I promise you that. Whatever I have can be yours too — if your unfathomable wealth isn't enough for you already, I mean."

“你在与人类之敌做生意吗？”
"Do you do business with the enemies of Humanity?"

"It has been known to happen. After years of dealing with xenos, I've learned their customs and even got a grasp of their language — except they cringe whenever I start speaking. Arrogant sods! They dislike even our voices, but they never turn away our valuables. Then again, I'm used to seeing sour faces — in this trade, the easily offended go out of business."

婕伊退了一步，哼了一声，似乎是被冒犯到了。“我们之间的关系，随便你怎么称呼都好，亲爱的。毕竟话语就像风一样，没有太大意义。但你曾对我照顾有加，所以我也希望能照顾到你……并稍微超出我们协议中的严格条款。收下吧，这是我带来的小礼物，带着我的感激之情。愿至高无上的神皇始终指引你的道路。”
Jae draws back and huffs, seemingly offended. "You are welcome to call our relations whatever you like, shereen. After all, words are wind and mean little. But you took good care of me, and so I would like to take care of you... and go slightly beyond the strict terms of our agreement. Here, I have brought a small gift as a token of gratitude. And may the Exalted One keep watching over the paths that you tread."

“你对我照顾有加，所以我也希望能照顾到你……并稍微超出我们协议中的严格条款。收下吧，这是我带来的小礼物，带着我的感激之情。愿至高无上的神皇始终指引你的道路。”

“在落脚港，这种事情没什么难的。我花了一年的时间为老好人克里斯托工作。他是个勇敢的士兵，和兽人混战的时候丧了命，于是我便接管了他的生意。只要保护好自己的脑袋别掉，把至高无上的神皇放在心里，就有助于迅速认识新的伙伴。到了最后，我聚集了一群诚实而忠诚的人。我仅仅做了几笔成功的交易，就引起了卡斯巴利卡的注意。很快，我便在落脚港安顿下来，将我的智慧传授给我的门徒与下属。到了那个时候，我已经不再需要亲自弄脏手了。”
"It's not hard to do on Footfall. I spent a year working for good old Cristo — he was a brave soldier who gave up the ghost in a scuffle with Orks — and then took over his business. Having a good head on your shoulders and keeping the Exalted One in your heart helps to establish new contacts quickly. Eventually I gathered together a group of honest and loyal people, and it only took a few successful contracts for the Kasballica to take notice. I quickly settled on Footfall and started dispensing my wisdom to my proteges and subordinates — I lost the taste for getting my hands dirty."

“和我介绍一下冷市贸易吧。”
"Tell me about the Cold Trade."

“实际上真的很简单，亲爱的。卡斯巴利卡经营着帝国的黑市，为那些能负担得起服务的人提供特别的商品。没错，我指的就是异形造物，包括外星武器与技术设备……有时甚至会包括某些……活着的东西。”
"It really is simple, shereen. The Kasballica runs the Imperium's black market, offering special goods to those who can afford their services. Yes, I am talking about xeno-artefacts, too — alien weapons, technology... Sometimes even certain kinds of... living creatures."

“行商浪人拥有神圣的授状，他们甚至可以忽视至高无上的神皇制定的律法。但卡斯巴利卡的代理人并非如此，他们习惯隐藏、掩盖他们的足迹。没人愿意引起不必要的注意，无论是谁的注意……尤其是这种时候，科罗努斯扩区迎来了一位黄金王座的战士，守望这片星区。”
"Unlike the Rogue Traders whose sacred Warrants make them immune even from the laws of the Exalted One, Kasballican agents are used to hiding and covering their tracks. Nobody wants to draw unwanted attention, no matter who might take an interest... Especially now that the Koronus Expanse has a warrior of the Golden Throne as its watchman."

"My trade means knowing the right people and non-people, having the right connections, and making sure the precious goods find their way into the hands of my no-less-precious customers. My wisdom includes the knowledge of the enemies of Humankind, be they xenos or the lowest scum in the Imperium, as well as the latest knowledge about how much they charge for any particular curio at the Footfall market. Not even the most cunning azhi will deceive you as long as I am with you, shereen — I promise you that. Whatever I have can be yours too — if your unfathomable wealth isn't enough for you already, I mean."

"It has been known to happen. After years of dealing with xenos, I've learned their customs and even got a grasp of their language — except they cringe whenever I start speaking. Arrogant sods! They dislike even our voices, but they never turn away our valuables. Then again, I'm used to seeing sour faces — in this trade, the easily offended go out of business."

Jae stops smiling and rubs the bridge of her nose wearily. "Listen, shereen, the giver of happiness and the dearest of my friends... I am who I am — a Cold Trader, a Kasballican agent, and your partner. We each have a past, and that past is sealed. I am not prying into your soul, am I? Well, have pity on mine, it has already been gnawed at by the azhi. And if you don't like the sound of that, we'll just go our separate ways, deal?"

I could purchase one of Footfall's asteroids, but not a planet. I could subjugate a few gangs from the shady districts, but not Vladaym! And so the answer to your question is no. I do not consider myself rich. I am not rich enough."

  • 选择 Choice

“你本可以当个甩手掌柜，坐享其成，可你为什么要踏上虚空舰，过着充满危险的生活？”
"You could be sitting back reaping the fruits of your own work, so why have you chosen to embrace the vicissitudes of life aboard a voidship?"

“你又何尝不是呢，{name}？”婕伊扬起了眉毛。“我已经厌倦了落脚港没完没了的合同与协议。这种事情我已经干了……多少年？但在这里，在群星之间，无论做什么都像是在刀尖上跳舞。没有什么事情比亚空间跳跃更刺激，更能令我兴奋，更不用提那些危机四伏的行星了。落脚港让我变得越来越脑满肠肥，亲爱的，我可不想变成那个样子。”

"I am but a fragile flower in your mighty hand, shereen. I can only give you what fragrance the Exalted One has granted me until you tire of me. Cast me aside, and let the scorching heat turn me into a desiccated sarcophagus for the sentiment that once lay between us."

  • 选择 Choice

“你明白我的意思了，很好。”
"So you understand. Good."

“婕伊·海达利会和危险的人、善变的人、以及行商浪人这样的人做生意。如果她不善解人意，她的人生恐怕会比老人嘴间袅袅升起麻烟还要苦涩。”
"Jae Heydari does business with dangerous people, mercurial people, people like the Rogue Trader. If she weren't understanding, her life would be more bitter than the lho smoke that curls out from between aged lips."

"Yes. To lose me, to be left with only the memories of Jae Heydari, sounds truly terrible. Who would wish to bear the stamp of such awful regret on their heart?"

"Then let us both be silent together about this beautiful feeling, shereen."

婕伊挥挥手，让你离开。“亲爱的，我们之间肯定曾擦出过火花，但现在已经消散了。我不愿指责你，但如果你真对我充满了兴趣，你会忽视我想要得到帝国官方行商执照的请求吗？不要满脑子想着很多事情本可能会是什么样子，亲爱的。我从你身上得到了很多好处，这足以让我永远对你感激不尽。不过，至高无上的神皇为我们安排的，也就到此为止了。”
Jae waves you off. "Shereen, there was definitely a spark between us, but it has faded. I'm not trying to point the finger, but would you have ignored my request for help in acquiring the Mercatum Tabula Officiale if you had had a burning interest in me? Don't fill your head with thoughts of what might have been, shereen. I have seen much good from you, and that is enough to earn my eternal gratitude. But the Exalted One has sent us no more than that."

“你好像对阿洁塔相当钟意，我说得对吗？”
"Argenta seems to have gotten under your skin. Am I right?"

“阿洁塔……”婕伊脸红了。“还有什么人能比战斗修女更加美妙呢？光是她的存在本身，就足以在我迷失灵魂的阴暗角落中洒下明光。但遗憾的是，我仅存的理智告诉我，可怜的婕伊只能欣赏这位天使的光芒，不能抱着任何不切实际的希望，渴望触碰她的翅膀。”
"Argenta..." The smuggler blushes. "What could be more beautiful than the sight of a Sister of Battle, whose mere presence casts light in the dark corners of lost souls such as mine? But alas, what remains of my sanity is telling me that poor Jae can only admire the radiance of this angel, forsaking any hope of ever touching her wings."

  • 选择 Choice

“你一直在说着我之前没怎么听过的词，比如‘亲爱的’。”
"You keep using words I don't understand. Like calling me 'shereen.'"

婕伊用手指捻起一缕乌黑的头发。“这些词来自我的故乡艾弗里特，与科罗努斯扩区的语言有很大区别。在我们的语言中，每个词都包含着很多种不同的含义。这样一来，我们的智者便可以充分阐释他们的深邃思想，而我们这些普通人则可以表达我们基本的激情与欲望。”
Jae starts to twist a strand of her raven black hair around her finger. "The language on Efreet, my homeworld, is quite different from the one spoken in the Koronus Expanse. We bestow more than one meaning upon each word, allowing our wise men to fully express their sagacious thoughts, and us, lowly dabblers, our base passions and desires."

“举个例子，比如‘鬼怪’这个词，我会用来称呼那些人渣与恶棍，因为这个词原本的意思是邪恶、敌人，以及毫无价值的可怜虫。再举个例子，比如‘坏种’这个词，它原本的意思是傻瓜，表弟，以及那些跌跌撞撞，若是失去指引便会掉进坑里的瞎子。至于‘亲爱的’……这个词指的是朋友、同志，以及生死与共的战友，正如你我一样，{name}。”
"Take 'azhi,' for example. That is what I call every piece of scum and villain, because 'azhi' means evil, and foe, and pathetic worm unworthy of consideration. Or take 'ashmag' — it means fool, and little brother, and blind man who stumbles and would fall into a pit without guidance. 'Shereen' is... 'shereen' means friend, and comrade, and rowmate in a battle formation — like we are, {name}."

“从我的船上下去。”
"Get off my ship."

婕伊难以置信地扬起了眉毛。“发生什么事情了，亲爱的？你已经厌倦了我的陪伴吗？”
Jae raises an eyebrow quizzically. "What happened, shereen? Have you grown tired of my company?"
